@import(\"args.zig\");\nconst test_util = @import(\"../test_util.zig\");\n\nconst Issue = models.Issue;\nconst CommandContext = common.CommandContext;\nconst DependencyGraph = common.DependencyGraph;\n\npub const ShowError = error{\n    WorkspaceNotInitialized,\n    IssueNotFound,\n    StorageError,\n    OutOfMemory,\n};\n\npub const ShowResult = struct {\n    success: ShowError.WorkspaceNotInitialized;\n    };\n    defer ctx.deinit();\n\n    const structured_output = global.isStructuredOutput();\n    var issue = (try ctx.store.getWithRelations(show_args.id)) orelse {\n        try common.outputNotFoundError(ShowResult, &ctx.output, structured_output, show_args.id, allocator);\n        return ShowError.IssueNotFound;\n    };\n    defer issue.deinit(allocator);\n\n u8 = null;\n\n        if (deps.len > 0) {\n            depends_on_ids = try allocator.alloc([]const u8, deps.len);\n            for (deps, 0..) |dep, i| {\n                depends_on_ids.?[i] = return .{\n    90→            .mode = mode,\n    91→            .toon = opts.toon,\n    92→            .stdout = stdout,\n    93→            .stderr = stderr,\n    94→            .allocator = allocator,\n    95→        };\n    96→    }\n    97→\n    98→    /// Initialize with explicit mode (useful for testing).\n    99→    pub fn initWithMode(allocator: std.mem.Allocator, mode: OutputMode) Self {\n   100→        return .{\n   101→            .mode = mode,\n   102→            .toon = false,\n   103→            .stdout = std.fs.File.stdout(),\n   104→            .stderr = std.fs.File.stderr(),\n   105→            .allocator = allocator,\n   106→        };\n   107→    }\n   108→\n   109→    /// Initialize for testing with custom file handles.\n   110→    pub fn initForTesting(allocator: std.mem.Allocator, mode: OutputMode, stdout: std.fs.File, stderr: std.fs.File) Self {\n   111→        return .{\n   112→            .mode = mode,\n   113→            .toon = false,\n   114→            .stdout = stdout,\n   115→            .stderr = stderr,\n   116→            .allocator = allocator,\n   117→        };\n   118→    }\n   119→\n   120→    // ========================================================================\n   121→    // Issue Display\n   122→    // ========================================================================\n   123→\n   124→    /// Print a single issue in the appropriate format.\n   125→    pub fn printIssue(self: *Self, issue: Issue) !void {\n   126→        switch (self.mode) {\n   127→            .json => try self.printIssueJson(issue),\n   128→            .quiet => try self.printIssueQuiet(issue),\n   129→            .rich => try self.printIssueRich(issue),\n   130→            .plain => try self.printIssuePlain(issue),\n   131→        }\n   132→    }\n   133→\n   134→    /// Print a list of issues in the appropriate format.\n   135→    pub fn printIssueList(self: *Self, issues: []const Issue) !void {\n   136→        switch (self.mode) {\n   137→            .json => try self.printIssueListJson(issues),\n   138→            .quiet => try self.printIssueListQuiet(issues),\n   139→            .rich => try self.printIssueListRich(issues),\n   140→            .plain => try self.printIssueListPlain(issues),\n   141→        }\n   142→    }\n   143→\n   144→    // ========================================================================\n   145→    // Generic Messages\n   146→    // ========================================================================\n   147→\n   148→    /// Print a formatted message to stdout.\n   149→    pub fn print(self: *Self, comptime fmt: []const u8, args: anytype) !void {\n   150→        if (self.mode == .quiet) return;\n   151→        const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(self.allocator, fmt, args);\n   152→        defer self.allocator.free(msg);\n   153→        try self.stdout.writeAll(msg);\n   154→    }\n   155→\n   156→    /// Print a formatted message to stdout with newline.\n   157→    pub fn println(self: *Self, comptime fmt: []const u8, args: anytype) !void {\n   158→        if (self.mode == .quiet) return;\n   159→        const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(self.allocator, fmt ++ \"\\n\", args);\n   160→        defer self.allocator.free(msg);\n   161→        try self.stdout.writeAll(msg);\n   162→    }\n   163→\n   164→    /// Print a success message (green in rich mode).\n   165→    pub fn success(self: *Self, comptime fmt: []const u8, args: anytype) !void {\n   166→        if (self.mode == .quiet) return;\n   167→        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stdout.writeAll(Color.green);\n   168→        const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(self.allocator, fmt, args);\n   169→        defer self.allocator.free(msg);\n   170→        try self.stdout.writeAll(msg);\n   171→        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stdout.writeAll(Color.reset);\n   172→        try self.stdout.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n   173→    }\n   174→\n   175→    /// Print an error message to stderr (red in rich mode).\n   176→    pub fn err(self: *Self, comptime fmt: []const u8, args: anytype) !void {\n   177→        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stderr.writeAll(Color.red);\n   178→        const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(self.allocator, \"error: \" ++ fmt, args);\n   179→        defer self.allocator.free(msg);\n   180→        try self.stderr.writeAll(msg);\n   181→        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stderr.writeAll(Color.reset);\n   182→        try self.stderr.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n   183→    }\n   184→\n   185→    /// Print a warning message to stderr (yellow in rich mode).\n   186→    pub fn warn(self: *Self, comptime fmt: []const u8, args: anytype) !void {\n   187→        if (self.mode == .quiet) return;\n   188→        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stderr.writeAll(Color.yellow);\n   189→        const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(self.allocator, \"warning: \" ++ fmt, args);\n   190→        defer self.allocator.free(msg);\n   191→        try self.stderr.writeAll(msg);\n   192→        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stderr.writeAll(Color.reset);\n   193→        try self.stderr.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n   194→    }\n   195→\n   196→    /// Print an info message (cyan in rich mode).\n   197→    pub fn info(self: *Self, comptime fmt: []const u8, args: anytype) !void {\n   198→        if (self.mode == .quiet) return;\n   199→        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stdout.writeAll(Color.cyan);\n   200→        const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(self.allocator, fmt, args);\n   201→        defer self.allocator.free(msg);\n   202→        try self.stdout.writeAll(msg);\n   203→        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stdout.writeAll(Color.reset);\n   204→        try self.stdout.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n   205→    }\n   206→\n   207→    /// Print raw bytes to stdout (bypasses mode checks).\n   208→    pub fn raw(self: *Self, bytes: []const u8) !void {\n   209→        try self.stdout.writeAll(bytes);\n   210→    }\n   211→\n   212→    /// Print raw JSON value to stdout (for JSON mode).\n   213→    /// If toon mode is enabled, converts JSON to TOON format for reduced token usage.\n   214→    pub fn printJson(self: *Self, value: anytype) !void {\n   215→        const json_bytes = try std.json.Stringify.valueAlloc(self.allocator, value, .{});\n   216→        defer self.allocator.free(json_bytes);\n   217→\n   218→        if (self.toon) {\n   219→            const toon = @import(\"toon_zig\");\n   220→            const toon_bytes = toon.jsonToToon(self.allocator, json_bytes) catch |convert_err| {\n   221→                try self.stderr.writeAll(\"error: failed to convert to TOON format\\n\");\n   222→                return convert_err;\n   223→            };\n   224→            defer self.allocator.free(toon_bytes);\n   225→            try self.stdout.writeAll(toon_bytes);\n   226→        } else {\n   227→            try self.stdout.writeAll(json_bytes);\n   228→        }\n   229→        try self.stdout.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n   230→    }\n   231→\n   232→    // ========================================================================\n   233→    // JSON Mode Helpers\n   234→    // ========================================================================\n   235→\n   236→    fn printIssueJson(self: *Self, issue: Issue) !void {\n   237→        try self.printJson(issue);\n   238→    }\n   239→\n   240→    fn printIssueListJson(self: *Self, issues: []const Issue) !void {\n   241→        try self.printJson(issues);\n   242→    }\n   243→\n   244→    // ========================================================================\n   245→    // Plain Mode Helpers\n   246→    // ========================================================================\n   247→\n   248→    fn printIssuePlain(self: *Self, issue: Issue) !void {\n   249→        try self.writeFormatted(\"ID: {s}\\n\", .{issue.id});\n   250→        try self.writeFormatted(\"Title: {s}\\n\", .{issue.title});\n   251→        try self.writeFormatted(\"Status: {s}\\n\", .{issue.status.toString()});\n   252→        try self.writeFormatted(\"Priority: {s}\\n\", .{issue.priority.toString()});\n   253→        try self.writeFormatted(\"Type: {s}\\n\", .{issue.issue_type.toString()});\n   254→\n   255→        if (issue.description) |desc| {\n   256→            try self.writeFormatted(\"Description: {s}\\n\", .{desc});\n   257→        }\n   258→        if (issue.assignee) |assignee| {\n   259→            try self.writeFormatted(\"Assignee: {s}\\n\", .{assignee});\n   260→        }\n   261→        if (issue.labels.len > 0) {\n   262→            try self.stdout.writeAll(\"Labels: \");\n   263→            for (issue.labels, 0..) |label, i| {\n   264→                if (i > 0) try self.stdout.writeAll(\", \");\n   265→                try self.stdout.writeAll(label);\n   266→            }\n   267→            try self.stdout.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n   268→        }\n   269→        if (issue.due_at.value) |due| {\n   270→            try self.writeFormatted(\"Due: {d}\\n\", .{due});\n   271→        }\n   272→\n   273→        try self.writeFormatted(\"Created: {d}\\n\", .{issue.created_at.value});\n   274→        try self.writeFormatted(\"Updated: {d}\\n\", .{issue.updated_at.value});\n   275→    }\n   276→\n   277→    fn printIssueListPlain(self: *Self, issues: []const Issue) !void {\n   278→        for (issues) |issue| {\n   279→            const status_abbrev = abbreviateStatus(issue.status);\n   280→            try self.writeFormatted(\"{s}  [{s}] {s}\\n\", .{\n   281→                issue.id,\n   282→                status_abbrev,\n   283→                issue.title,\n   284→            });\n   285→        }\n   286→    }\n   287→\n   288→    // ========================================================================\n   289→    // Rich Mode Helpers (ANSI colors)\n   290→    // ========================================================================\n   291→\n   292→    fn printIssueRich(self: *Self, issue: Issue) !void {\n   293→        // Bold ID\n   294→        try self.writeFormatted(\"{s}{s}{s}\\n\", .{ Color.bold, issue.id, Color.reset });\n   295→\n   296→        // Title\n   297→        try self.writeFormatted(\"  {s}\\n\", .{issue.title});\n   298→\n   299→        // Status with color\n   300→        const status_color = getStatusColor(issue.status);\n   301→        try self.writeFormatted(\"  Status: {s}{s}{s}\\n\", .{ status_color, issue.status.toString(), Color.reset });\n   302→\n   303→        // Priority with color\n   304→        const priority_color = getPriorityColor(issue.priority);\n   305→        try self.writeFormatted(\"  Priority: {s}{s}{s}\\n\", .{ priority_color, issue.priority.toString(), Color.reset });\n   306→\n   307→        // Type\n   308→        try self.writeFormatted(\"  Type: {s}\\n\", .{issue.issue_type.toString()});\n   309→\n   310→        // Optional fields\n   311→        if (issue.description) |desc| {\n   312→            try self.writeFormatted(\"  Description: {s}{s}{s}\\n\", .{ Color.dim, desc, Color.reset });\n   313→        }\n   314→        if (issue.assignee) |assignee| {\n   315→            try self.writeFormatted(\"  Assignee: {s}{s}{s}\\n\", .{ Color.cyan, assignee, Color.reset });\n   316→        }\n   317→        if (issue.labels.len > 0) {\n   318→            try self.stdout.writeAll(\"  Labels: \");\n   319→            for (issue.labels, 0..) |label, i| {\n   320→                if (i > 0) try self.stdout.writeAll(\", \");\n   321→                try self.writeFormatted(\"{s}{s}{s}\", .{ Color.magenta, label, Color.reset });\n   322→            }\n   323→            try self.stdout.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n   324→        }\n   325→    }\n   326→\n   327→    fn printIssueListRich(self: *Self, issues: []const Issue) !void {\n   328→        for (issues) |issue| {\n   329→            const status_color = getStatusColor(issue.status);\n   330→            const priority_color = getPriorityColor(issue.priority);\n   331→            const status_abbrev = abbreviateStatus(issue.status);\n   332→\n   333→            try self.writeFormatted(\"{s}{s}{s}  {s}[{s}]{s}  {s}{s}{s}  {s}\\n\", .{\n   334→                Color.bold,\n   335→                issue.id,\n   336→                Color.reset,\n   337→                status_color,\n   338→                status_abbrev,\n   339→                Color.reset,\n   340→                priority_color,\n   341→                priorityIndicator(issue.priority),\n   342→                Color.reset,\n   343→                issue.title,\n   344→            });\n   345→        }\n   346→    }\n   347→\n   348→    // ========================================================================\n   349→    // Quiet Mode Helpers\n   350→    // ========================================================================\n   351→\n   352→    fn printIssueQuiet(self: *Self, issue: Issue) !void {\n   353→        try self.writeFormatted(\"{s}\\n\", .{issue.id});\n   354→    }\n   355→\n   356→    fn printIssueListQuiet(self: *Self, issues: []const Issue) !void {\n   357→        for (issues) |issue| {\n   358→            try self.writeFormatted(\"{s}\\n\", .{issue.id});\n   359→        }\n   360→    }\n   361→\n   362→    // ========================================================================\n   363→    // Internal Helpers\n   364→    // ========================================================================\n   365→\n   366→    fn writeFormatted(self: *Self, comptime fmt: []const u8, args: anytype) !void {\n   367→        const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(self.allocator, fmt, args);\n   368→        defer self.allocator.free(msg);\n   369→        try self.stdout.writeAll(msg);\n   370→    }\n   371→};\n   372→\n   373→// ============================================================================\n   374→// Helper Functions\n   375→// ============================================================================\n   376→\n   377→/// Check if NO_COLOR environment variable is set (cross-platform).\n   378→fn checkNoColorEnv() bool {\n   379→    // Per NO_COLOR spec, only existence matters, not the value\n   380→    return std.process.hasEnvVarConstant(\"NO_COLOR\");\n   381→}\n   382→\n   383→/// Get ANSI color for a status.\n   384→fn getStatusColor(status: Status) []const u8 {\n   385→    return switch (status) {\n   386→        .open => Color.green,\n   387→        .in_progress => Color.yellow,\n   388→        .blocked => Color.red,\n   389→        .deferred => Color.gray,\n   390→        .closed => Color.gray,\n   391→        .tombstone => Color.dim,\n   392→        .pinned => Color.bright_cyan,\n   393→        .custom => Color.blue,\n   394→    };\n   395→}\n   396→\n   397→/// Get ANSI color for a priority.\n   398→fn getPriorityColor(priority: Priority) []const u8 {\n   399→    return switch (priority.value) {\n   400→        0 => Color.bright_red, // critical\n   401→        1 => Color.red, // high\n   402→        2 => Color.yellow, // medium\n   403→        3 => Color.green, // low\n   404→        4 => Color.gray, // backlog\n   405→        else => Color.reset,\n   406→    };\n   407→}\n   408→\n   409→/// Get short status abbreviation.\n   410→fn abbreviateStatus(status: Status) []const u8 {\n   411→    return switch (status) {\n   412→        .open => \"OPEN\",\n   413→        .in_progress => \"PROG\",\n   414→        .blocked => \"BLKD\",\n   415→        .deferred => \"DEFR\",\n   416→        .closed => \"DONE\",\n   417→        .tombstone => \"DEL \",\n   418→        .pinned => \"PIN \",\n   419→        .custom => \"CUST\",\n   420→    };\n   421→}\n   422→\n   423→/// Get priority indicator symbol.\n   424→fn priorityIndicator(priority: Priority) []const u8 {\n   425→    return switch (priority.value) {\n   426→        0 => \"!!!\",\n   427→        1 => \"!! \",\n   428→        2 => \"!  \",\n   429→        3 => \".  \",\n   430→        4 => \"   \",\n   431→        else => \"   \",\n   432→    };\n   433→}\n   434→\n   435→// ============================================================================\n   436→// Tests\n   437→// ============================================================================\n   438→\n   439→test \"OutputMode enum values\" {\n   440→    try std.testing.expectEqual(OutputMode.plain, OutputMode.plain);\n   441→    try std.testing.expectEqual(OutputMode.rich, OutputMode.rich);\n   442→    try std.testing.expectEqual(OutputMode.json, OutputMode.json);\n   443→    try std.testing.expectEqual(OutputMode.quiet, OutputMode.quiet);\n   444→}\n   445→\n   446→test \"Output.init with json option\" {\n   447→    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n   448→    const opts = OutputOptions{ .json = true };\n   449→    const output = Output.init(allocator, opts);\n   450→    try std.testing.expectEqual(OutputMode.json, output.mode);\n   451→    try std.testing.expect(!output.toon);\n   452→}\n   453→\n   454→test \"Output.init with toon option\" {\n   455→    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n   456→    const opts = OutputOptions{ .toon = true };\n   457→    const output = Output.init(allocator, opts);\n   458→    try std.testing.expectEqual(OutputMode.json, output.mode);\n   459→    try std.testing.expect(output.toon);\n   460→}\n   461→\n   462→test \"Output.init with quiet option\" {\n   463→    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n   464→    const opts = OutputOptions{ .quiet = true };\n   465→    const output = Output.init(allocator, opts);\n   466→    try std.testing.expectEqual(OutputMode.quiet, output.mode);\n   467→}\n   468→\n   469→test \"Output.init with no_color option forces plain mode\" {\n   470→    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n   471→    const opts = OutputOptions{ .no_color = true };\n   472→    const output = Output.init(allocator, opts);\n   473→    try std.testing.expectEqual(OutputMode.plain, output.mode);\n   474→}\n   475→\n   476→test \"Output.init json overrides quiet\" {\n   477→    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n   478→    const opts = OutputOptions{ .json = true, .quiet = true };\n   479→    const output = Output.init(allocator, opts);\n   480→    try std.testing.expectEqual(OutputMode.json, output.mode);\n   481→}\n   482→\n   483→test \"Output.initWithMode sets explicit mode\" {\n   484→    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n   485→    const output = Output.initWithMode(allocator, .rich);\n   486→    try std.testing.expectEqual(OutputMode.rich, output.mode);\n   487→}\n   488→\n   489→test \"abbreviateStatus returns 4-char strings\" {\n   490→    const statuses = [_]Status{\n   491→        .open,\n   492→        .in_progress,\n   493→        .blocked,\n   494→        .deferred,\n   495→        .closed,\n   496→        .tombstone,\n   497→        .pinned,\n   498→        .{ .custom = \"test\" },\n   499→    };\n   500→    for (statuses) |status| {\n   501→        const abbrev = abbreviateStatus(status);\n   502→        try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 4), abbrev.len);\n   503→    }\n   504→}\n   505→\n   506→test \"priorityIndicator returns 3-char strings\" {\n   507→    var p: u3 = 0;\n   508→    while (p <= 4) : (p += 1) {\n   509→        const priority = Priority{ .value = p };\n   510→        const indicator = priorityIndicator(priority);\n   511→        try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 3), indicator.len);\n   512→    }\n   513→}\n   514→\n   515→test \"getStatusColor returns valid ANSI codes\" {\n   516→    const statuses = [_]Status{\n   517→        .open,\n   518→        .in_progress,\n   519→        .blocked,\n   520→        .deferred,\n   521→        .closed,\n   522→        .tombstone,\n   523→        .pinned,\n   524→        .{ .custom = \"test\" },\n   525→    };\n   526→    for (statuses) |status| {\n   527→        const color = getStatusColor(status);\n   528→        try std.testing.expect(color.len > 0);\n   529→        try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, color, \"\\x1b[\"));\n   530→    }\n   531→}\n   532→\n   533→test \"getPriorityColor returns valid ANSI codes\" {\n   534→    var p: u3 = 0;\n   535→    while (p <= 4) : (p += 1) {\n   536→        const priority = Priority{ .value = p };\n   537→        const color = getPriorityColor(priority);\n   538→        try std.testing.expect(color.len > 0);\n   539→        try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, color, \"\\x1b[\"));\n   540→    }\n   541→}\n   542→\n   543→test \"Color constants are valid ANSI escape sequences\" {\n   544→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, Color.reset, \"\\x1b[\"));\n   545→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, Color.bold, \"\\x1b[\"));\n   546→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, Color.red, \"\\x1b[\"));\n   547→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, Color.green, \"\\x1b[\"));\n   548→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, Color.yellow, \"\\x1b[\"));\n   549→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, Color.blue, \"\\x1b[\"));\n   550→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, Color.gray, \"\\x1b[\"));\n   551→}\n   552→\n   553→test \"Output printIssueListQuiet writes IDs only\" {\n   554→    // Test the quiet formatting logic directly\n   555→    const issue1 = Issue.init(\"bd-abc123\", \"Test issue 1\", 1706540000);\n   556→    const issue2 = Issue.init(\"bd-def456\", \"Test issue 2\", 1706540000);\n   557→    const issues = [_]Issue{ issue1, issue2 };\n   558→\n   559→    // In quiet mode, printIssueListQuiet outputs \"{id}\\n\" for each issue\n   560→    // Verify the expected output format\n   561→    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"bd-abc123\", issue1.id);\n   562→    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"bd-def456\", issue2.id);\n   563→    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 2), issues.len);\n   564→}\n   565→\n   566→test \"Output printIssueListPlain writes formatted lines\" {\n   567→    // Test the plain formatting logic via abbreviateStatus and Issue fields\n   568→    const issue = Issue.init(\"bd-abc123\", \"Test issue\", 1706540000);\n   569→\n   570→    // Verify issue fields are correct\n   571→    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"bd-abc123\", issue.id);\n   572→    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"Test issue\", issue.title);\n   573→    try std.testing.expectEqual(Status.open, issue.status);\n   574→\n   575→    // Verify status abbreviation\n   576→    const status_abbrev = abbreviateStatus(issue.status);\n   577→    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"OPEN\", status_abbrev);\n   578→}\n   579→\n   580→test \"Output printIssueListRich includes ANSI codes\" {\n   581→    // Test that rich mode formatting uses ANSI codes\n   582→    const issue = Issue.init(\"bd-abc123\", \"Test issue\", 1706540000);\n   583→\n   584→    // Verify issue fields\n   585→    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"bd-abc123\", issue.id);\n   586→\n   587→    // Verify rich mode uses color codes\n   588→    const status_color = getStatusColor(issue.status);\n   589→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, status_color, \"\\x1b[\"));\n   590→\n   591→    const priority_color = getPriorityColor(issue.priority);\n   592→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, priority_color, \"\\x1b[\"));\n   593→\n   594→    // Verify Color.bold is used\n   595→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, Color.bold, \"\\x1b[\"));\n   596→}\n   597→\n   598→test \"Output printIssueListJson produces valid JSON array\" {\n   599→    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n   600→\n   601→    // Test JSON serialization directly\n   602→    const issue1 = Issue.init(\"bd-abc123\", \"Test issue 1\", 1706540000);\n   603→    const issue2 = Issue.init(\"bd-def456\", \"Test issue 2\", 1706540000);\n   604→    const issues = [_]Issue{ issue1, issue2 };\n   605→\n   606→    // Serialize to JSON\n   607→    const json_bytes = try std.json.Stringify.valueAlloc(allocator, issues, .{});\n   608→    defer allocator.free(json_bytes);\n   609→\n   610→    // Verify it starts with [ and contains expected data\n   611→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, json_bytes, \"[\"));\n   612→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.indexOf(u8, json_bytes, \"bd-abc123\") != null);\n   613→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.indexOf(u8, json_bytes, \"bd-def456\") != null);\n   614→\n   615→    // Verify it can be parsed back\n   616→    const parsed = try std.json.parseFromSlice([]const Issue, allocator, json_bytes, .{});\n   617→    defer parsed.deinit();\n   618→    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 2), parsed.value.len);\n   619→}\n   620→\n   621→test \"Output.err formats error messages correctly\" {\n   622→    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n Output formatting for beads_zig.\n//!\n//! Provides a unified interface for displaying output in different modes:\n//! - plain: No colors, basic formatting (default for non-TTY)\n//! - rich: Colors and formatting (default for TTY)\n//! - json: Structured JSON output for machine consumption\n//! - quiet: Minimal output (IDs only)\n//!\n//! Respects NO_COLOR environment variable and --no-color flag.\n\nconst std = @import(\"std\");\nconst models = @import(\"../models/mod.zig\");\nconst Issue = models.Issue;\nconst Status = models.Status;\nconst Priority = models.Priority;\nconst IssueType = models.IssueType;\n\n/// Output mode determines formatting and verbosity.\npub const OutputMode = enum {\n    plain, // No colors, basic formatting\n    rich, // Colors and formatting (TTY)\n    json, // Structured JSON output\n    quiet, // Minimal output (IDs only)\n};\n\n/// ANSI color escape codes.\npub const Color = struct {\n    pub const reset = \"\\x1b[0m\";\n    pub const bold = \"\\x1b[1m\";\n    pub const dim = \"\\x1b[2m\";\n    pub const italic = \"\\x1b[3m\";\n    pub const underline = \"\\x1b[4m\";\n\n    pub const red = \"\\x1b[31m\";\n    pub const green = \"\\x1b[32m\";\n    pub const yellow = \"\\x1b[33m\";\n    pub const blue = \"\\x1b[34m\";\n    pub const magenta = \"\\x1b[35m\";\n    pub const cyan = \"\\x1b[36m\";\n    pub const white = \"\\x1b[37m\";\n    pub const gray = \"\\x1b[90m\";\n\n    pub const bright_red = \"\\x1b[91m\";\n    pub const bright_green = \"\\x1b[92m\";\n    pub const bright_yellow = \"\\x1b[93m\";\n    pub const bright_blue = \"\\x1b[94m\";\n    pub const bright_magenta = \"\\x1b[95m\";\n    pub const bright_cyan = \"\\x1b[96m\";\n\n    pub const bg_red = \"\\x1b[41m\";\n    pub const bg_green = \"\\x1b[42m\";\n    pub const bg_yellow = \"\\x1b[43m\";\n    pub const bg_blue = \"\\x1b[44m\";\n};\n\n/// Global options that affect output formatting.\n/// This mirrors the relevant fields from cli.args.GlobalOptions.\npub const OutputOptions = struct {\n    json: bool = false,\n    toon: bool = false,\n    quiet: bool = false,\n    no_color: bool = false,\n};\n\n/// Output formatter for consistent CLI output across all modes.\npub const Output = struct {\n    mode: OutputMode,\n    toon: bool,\n    stdout: std.fs.File,\n    stderr: std.fs.File,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n\n    const Self = @This();\n\n    /// Initialize output formatter based on global options and TTY detection.\n    pub fn init(allocator: std.mem.Allocator, opts: OutputOptions) Self {\n        const stdout = std.fs.File.stdout();\n        const stderr = std.fs.File.stderr();\n\n        var mode: OutputMode = .plain;\n        if (opts.json or opts.toon) {\n            mode = .json;\n        } else if (opts.quiet) {\n            mode = .quiet;\n        } else if (!opts.no_color and !checkNoColorEnv() and stdout.isTty()) {\n            mode = .rich;\n        }\n\n        return .{\n            .mode = mode,\n            .toon = opts.toon,\n            .stdout = stdout,\n            .stderr = stderr,\n            .allocator = allocator,\n        };\n    }\n\n    /// Initialize with explicit mode (useful for testing).\n    pub fn initWithMode(allocator: std.mem.Allocator, mode: OutputMode) Self {\n        return .{\n            .mode = mode,\n            .toon = false,\n            .stdout = std.fs.File.stdout(),\n            .stderr = std.fs.File.stderr(),\n            .allocator = allocator,\n        };\n    }\n\n    /// Initialize for testing with custom file handles.\n    pub fn initForTesting(allocator: std.mem.Allocator, mode: OutputMode, stdout: std.fs.File, stderr: std.fs.File) Self {\n        return .{\n            .mode = mode,\n            .toon = false,\n            .stdout = stdout,\n            .stderr = stderr,\n            .allocator = allocator,\n        };\n    }\n\n    // ========================================================================\n    // Issue Display\n    // ========================================================================\n\n    /// Print a single issue in the appropriate format.\n    pub fn printIssue(self: *Self, issue: Issue) !void {\n        switch (self.mode) {\n            .json => try self.printIssueJson(issue),\n            .quiet => try self.printIssueQuiet(issue),\n            .rich => try self.printIssueRich(issue),\n            .plain => try self.printIssuePlain(issue),\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Print a list of issues in the appropriate format.\n    pub fn printIssueList(self: *Self, issues: []const Issue) !void {\n        switch (self.mode) {\n            .json => try self.printIssueListJson(issues),\n            .quiet => try self.printIssueListQuiet(issues),\n            .rich => try self.printIssueListRich(issues),\n            .plain => try self.printIssueListPlain(issues),\n        }\n    }\n\n    // ========================================================================\n    // Generic Messages\n    // ========================================================================\n\n    /// Print a formatted message to stdout.\n    pub fn print(self: *Self, comptime fmt: []const u8, args: anytype) !void {\n        if (self.mode == .quiet) return;\n        const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(self.allocator, fmt, args);\n        defer self.allocator.free(msg);\n        try self.stdout.writeAll(msg);\n    }\n\n    /// Print a formatted message to stdout with newline.\n    pub fn println(self: *Self, comptime fmt: []const u8, args: anytype) !void {\n        if (self.mode == .quiet) return;\n        const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(self.allocator, fmt ++ \"\\n\", args);\n        defer self.allocator.free(msg);\n        try self.stdout.writeAll(msg);\n    }\n\n    /// Print a success message (green in rich mode).\n    pub fn success(self: *Self, comptime fmt: []const u8, args: anytype) !void {\n        if (self.mode == .quiet) return;\n        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stdout.writeAll(Color.green);\n        const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(self.allocator, fmt, args);\n        defer self.allocator.free(msg);\n        try self.stdout.writeAll(msg);\n        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stdout.writeAll(Color.reset);\n        try self.stdout.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n    }\n\n    /// Print an error message to stderr (red in rich mode).\n    pub fn err(self: *Self, comptime fmt: []const u8, args: anytype) !void {\n        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stderr.writeAll(Color.red);\n        const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(self.allocator, \"error: \" ++ fmt, args);\n        defer self.allocator.free(msg);\n        try self.stderr.writeAll(msg);\n        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stderr.writeAll(Color.reset);\n        try self.stderr.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n    }\n\n    /// Print a warning message to stderr (yellow in rich mode).\n    pub fn warn(self: *Self, comptime fmt: []const u8, args: anytype) !void {\n        if (self.mode == .quiet) return;\n        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stderr.writeAll(Color.yellow);\n        const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(self.allocator, \"warning: \" ++ fmt, args);\n        defer self.allocator.free(msg);\n        try self.stderr.writeAll(msg);\n        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stderr.writeAll(Color.reset);\n        try self.stderr.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n    }\n\n    /// Print an info message (cyan in rich mode).\n    pub fn info(self: *Self, comptime fmt: []const u8, args: anytype) !void {\n        if (self.mode == .quiet) return;\n        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stdout.writeAll(Color.cyan);\n        const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(self.allocator, fmt, args);\n        defer self.allocator.free(msg);\n        try self.stdout.writeAll(msg);\n        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stdout.writeAll(Color.reset);\n        try self.stdout.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n    }\n\n    /// Print raw bytes to stdout (bypasses mode checks).\n    pub fn raw(self: *Self, bytes: []const u8) !void {\n        try self.stdout.writeAll(bytes);\n    }\n\n    /// Print raw JSON value to stdout (for JSON mode).\n    /// If toon mode is enabled, converts JSON to TOON format for reduced token usage.\n    pub fn printJson(self: *Self, value: anytype) !void {\n        const json_bytes = try std.json.Stringify.valueAlloc(self.allocator, value, .{});\n        defer self.allocator.free(json_bytes);\n\n        if (self.toon) {\n            const toon = @import(\"toon_zig\");\n            const toon_bytes = toon.jsonToToon(self.allocator, json_bytes) catch |convert_err| {\n                try self.stderr.writeAll(\"error: failed to convert to TOON format\\n\");\n                return convert_err;\n            };\n            defer self.allocator.free(toon_bytes);\n            try self.stdout.writeAll(toon_bytes);\n        } else {\n            try self.stdout.writeAll(json_bytes);\n        }\n        try self.stdout.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n    }\n\n    // ========================================================================\n    // JSON Mode Helpers\n    // ========================================================================\n\n    fn printIssueJson(self: *Self, issue: Issue) !void {\n        try self.printJson(issue);\n    }\n\n    fn printIssueListJson(self: *Self, issues: []const Issue) !void {\n        try self.printJson(issues);\n    }\n\n    // ========================================================================\n    // Plain Mode Helpers\n    // ========================================================================\n\n    fn printIssuePlain(self: *Self, issue: Issue) !void {\n        try self.writeFormatted(\"ID: {s}\\n\", .{issue.id});\n        try self.writeFormatted(\"Title: {s}\\n\", .{issue.title});\n        try self.writeFormatted(\"Status: {s}\\n\", .{issue.status.toString()});\n        try self.writeFormatted(\"Priority: {s}\\n\", .{issue.priority.toString()});\n        try self.writeFormatted(\"Type: {s}\\n\", .{issue.issue_type.toString()});\n\n        if (issue.description) |desc| {\n            try self.writeFormatted(\"Description: {s}\\n\", .{desc});\n        }\n        if (issue.assignee) |assignee| {\n            try self.writeFormatted(\"Assignee: {s}\\n\", .{assignee});\n        }\n        if (issue.labels.len > 0) {\n            try self.stdout.writeAll(\"Labels: \");\n            for (issue.labels, 0..) |label, i| {\n                if (i > 0) try self.stdout.writeAll(\", \");\n                try self.stdout.writeAll(label);\n            }\n            try self.stdout.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n        }\n        if (issue.due_at.value) |due| {\n            try self.writeFormatted(\"Due: {d}\\n\", .{due});\n        }\n\n        try self.writeFormatted(\"Created: {d}\\n\", .{issue.created_at.value});\n        try self.writeFormatted(\"Updated: {d}\\n\", .{issue.updated_at.value});\n    }\n\n    fn printIssueListPlain(self: *Self, issues: []const Issue) !void {\n        for (issues) |issue| {\n            const status_abbrev = abbreviateStatus(issue.status);\n            try self.writeFormatted(\"{s}  [{s}] {s}\\n\", .{\n                issue.id,\n                status_abbrev,\n                issue.title,\n            });\n        }\n    }\n\n    // ========================================================================\n    // Rich Mode Helpers (ANSI colors)\n    // ========================================================================\n\n    fn printIssueRich(self: *Self, issue: Issue) !void {\n        // Bold ID\n        try self.writeFormatted(\"{s}{s}{s}\\n\", .{ Color.bold, issue.id, Color.reset });\n\n        // Title\n        try self.writeFormatted(\"  {s}\\n\", .{issue.title});\n\n        // Status with color\n        const status_color = getStatusColor(issue.status);\n        try self.writeFormatted(\"  Status: {s}{s}{s}\\n\", .{ status_color, issue.status.toString(), Color.reset });\n\n        // Priority with color\n        const priority_color = getPriorityColor(issue.priority);\n        try self.writeFormatted(\"  Priority: {s}{s}{s}\\n\", .{ priority_color, issue.priority.toString(), Color.reset });\n\n        // Type\n        try self.writeFormatted(\"  Type: {s}\\n\", .{issue.issue_type.toString()});\n\n        // Optional fields\n        if (issue.description) |desc| {\n            try self.writeFormatted(\"  Description: {s}{s}{s}\\n\", .{ Color.dim, desc, Color.reset });\n        }\n        if (issue.assignee) |assignee| {\n            try self.writeFormatted(\"  Assignee: {s}{s}{s}\\n\", .{ Color.cyan, assignee, Color.reset });\n        }\n        if (issue.labels.len > 0) {\n            try self.stdout.writeAll(\"  Labels: \");\n            for (issue.labels, 0..) |label, i| {\n                if (i > 0) try self.stdout.writeAll(\", \");\n                try self.writeFormatted(\"{s}{s}{s}\", .{ Color.magenta, label, Color.reset });\n            }\n            try self.stdout.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n        }\n    }\n\n    fn printIssueListRich(self: *Self, issues: []const Issue) !void {\n        for (issues) |issue| {\n            const status_color = getStatusColor(issue.status);\n            const priority_color = getPriorityColor(issue.priority);\n            const status_abbrev = abbreviateStatus(issue.status);\n\n            try self.writeFormatted(\"{s}{s}{s}  {s}[{s}]{s}  {s}{s}{s}  {s}\\n\", .{\n                Color.bold,\n                issue.id,\n                Color.reset,\n                status_color,\n                status_abbrev,\n                Color.reset,\n                priority_color,\n                priorityIndicator(issue.priority),\n                Color.reset,\n                issue.title,\n            });\n        }\n    }\n\n    // ========================================================================\n    // Quiet Mode Helpers\n    // ========================================================================\n\n    fn printIssueQuiet(self: *Self, issue: Issue) !void {\n        try self.writeFormatted(\"{s}\\n\", .{issue.id});\n    }\n\n    fn printIssueListQuiet(self: *Self, issues: []const Issue) !void {\n        for (issues) |issue| {\n            try self.writeFormatted(\"{s}\\n\", .{issue.id});\n        }\n    }\n\n    // ========================================================================\n    // Internal Helpers\n    // ========================================================================\n\n    fn writeFormatted(self: *Self, comptime fmt: []const u8, args: anytype) !void {\n        const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(self.allocator, fmt, args);\n        defer self.allocator.free(msg);\n        try self.stdout.writeAll(msg);\n    }\n};\n\n// ============================================================================\n// Helper Functions\n// ============================================================================\n\n/// Check if NO_COLOR environment variable is set (cross-platform).\nfn checkNoColorEnv() bool {\n    // Per NO_COLOR spec, only existence matters, not the value\n    return std.process.hasEnvVarConstant(\"NO_COLOR\");\n}\n\n/// Get ANSI color for a status.\nfn getStatusColor(status: Status) []const u8 {\n    return switch (status) {\n        .open => Color.green,\n        .in_progress => Color.yellow,\n        .blocked => Color.red,\n        .deferred => Color.gray,\n        .closed => Color.gray,\n        .tombstone => Color.dim,\n        .pinned => Color.bright_cyan,\n        .custom => Color.blue,\n    };\n}\n\n/// Get ANSI color for a priority.\nfn getPriorityColor(priority: Priority) []const u8 {\n    return switch (priority.value) {\n        0 => Color.bright_red, // critical\n        1 => Color.red, // high\n        2 => Color.yellow, // medium\n        3 => Color.green, // low\n        4 => Color.gray, // backlog\n        else => Color.reset,\n    };\n}\n\n/// Get short status abbreviation.\nfn abbreviateStatus(status: Status) []const u8 {\n    return switch (status) {\n        .open => \"OPEN\",\n        .in_progress => \"PROG\",\n        .blocked => \"BLKD\",\n        .deferred => \"DEFR\",\n        .closed => \"DONE\",\n        .tombstone => \"DEL \",\n        .pinned => \"PIN \",\n        .custom => \"CUST\",\n    };\n}\n\n/// Get priority indicator symbol.\nfn priorityIndicator(priority: Priority) []const u8 {\n    return switch (priority.value) {\n        0 => \"!!!\",\n        1 => \"!! \",\n        2 => \"!  \",\n        3 => \".  \",\n        4 => \"   \",\n        else => \"   \",\n    };\n}\n\n// ============================================================================\n// Tests\n// ============================================================================\n\ntest \"OutputMode enum values\" {\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(OutputMode.plain, OutputMode.plain);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(OutputMode.rich, OutputMode.rich);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(OutputMode.json, OutputMode.json);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(OutputMode.quiet, OutputMode.quiet);\n}\n\ntest \"Output.init with json option\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n    const opts = OutputOptions{ .json = true };\n    const output = Color.red, \"\\x1b[\"));\n    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, Color.green, \"\\x1b[\"));\n    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, Color.yellow, \"\\x1b[\"));\n    try 323→    UnknownFlag,\n   324→    MissingFlagValue,\n   325→    InvalidShell,\n   326→    UnknownSubcommand,\n   327→};\n   328→\n   329→/// Command-line argument parser.\n   330→pub const ArgParser =   }\n   343→\n   344→    /// Parse all arguments into a ParseResult.\n   345→    pub fn parse(self: *Self) ParseError!ParseResult {\n   346→        var global = GlobalOptions{};\n   347→\n   348→        // Parse global flags first\n   349→        while (self.hasNext()) {\n   350→            const arg = self.peek().?;\n   351→            if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, arg, \"-\")) {\n   352→                if (self.parseGlobalFlag(&global)) |consumed| {\n   353→                    if (!consumed) break;\n   354→                } else |_| {\n   355→                    break;\n   356→                }\n   357→            } else {\n   358→                break;\n   359→            }\n   360→        }\n   361→\n   362→        // Parse subcommand\n   363→        const cmd_str = self.next() orelse {\n   364→            return .{\n   365→                .global = global,\n   366→                .command = .{ .help = .{ .topic = null } },\n   367→            };\n   368→        };\n   369→\n   370→        const command = try self.parseCommand(cmd_str);\n   371→\n   372→        return .{\n   373→            .global = global,\n   374→            .command = command,\n   375→        };\n   376→    }\n   377→\n   378→    fn parseGlobalFlag(self: *Self, global: *GlobalOptions) ParseError!bool {\n   379→        const arg = self.next().?;\n   380→\n   381→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--json\")) {\n   382→            global.json = true;\n   383→            return true;\n   384→        }\n   385→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--toon\")) {\n   386→            global.toon = true;\n   387→            return true;\n   388→        }\n   389→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"-q\") or std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--quiet\")) {\n   390→            global.quiet = true;\n   391→            return true;\n   392→        }\n   393→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"-v\") or std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--verbose\")) {\n   394→            global.verbose +|= 1;\n   395→            return true;\n   396→        }\n   397→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"-vv\")) {\n   398→            global.verbose +|= 2;\n   399→            return true;\n   400→        }\n   401→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--no-color\")) {\n   402→            global.no_color = true;\n   403→            return true;\n   404→        }\n   405→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--no-auto-flush\")) {\n   406→            global.no_auto_flush = true;\n   407→            return true;\n   408→        }\n   409→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--no-auto-import\")) {\n   410→            global.no_auto_import = true;\n   411→            return true;\n   412→        }\n   413→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--data\") or std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--db\")) {\n   414→            global.data_path = self.next() orelse error.MissingFlagValue;\n   419→            return true;\n   420→        }\n   421→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--lock-timeout\")) {\n   422→            const val = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n   423→            global.lock_timeout = std.fmt.parseInt(u32, val, 10) catch return error.InvalidArgument;\n   424→            return true;\n   425→        }\n   426→\n   427→        // Put back if not recognized\n   428→        self.index -= 1;\n   429→        return error.UnknownFlag;\n   430→    }\n   431→\n   432→    fn parseCommand(self: *Self, cmd: []const u8) ParseError!Command {\n   433→        // Workspace\n   434→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"init\")) {\n   435→            return .{ .init = try self.parseInitArgs() };\n   436→        }\n   437→ 447→            return .{ .config = try self.parseConfigArgs() };\n   448→        }\n   449→\n   450→        // Issue CRUD\n   451→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"create\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"edit\")) {\n   461→            return .{ .update = try self.parseUpdateArgs() };\n   462→        }\n   463→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"close\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"done\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"finish\")) {\n   464→            return .{ .close = try self.parseCloseArgs() };\n   465→        }\n   466→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"reopen\")) {\n   467→            return .{ .reopen = try self.parseReopenArgs() };\n   468→        }\n   469→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"delete\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"rm\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"remove\")) {\n   470→            return .{ .delete = try self.parseDeleteArgs() };\n   471→        }\n   472→\n   473→        // Query\n   474→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"list\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"ls\")) {\n      if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"search\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"find\")) {\n   484→            return .{ .search = try self.parseSearchArgs() };\n   485→        }\n   486→        if       return self.index < self.args.len;\n   894→    }\n   895→\n   896→    fn peek(self: *Self) ?[]const u8 {\n   897→        if (self.index >= self.args.len) return null;\n   898→        return self.args[self.index];\n   899→    }\n   900→\n   901→    fn next(self: *Self) ?[]const u8 {\n   902→        if (self.index >= self.args.len) return null;\n   903→        const arg = self.args[self.index];\n   904→        self.index += 1;\n   905→        return arg;\n   906→    }\n   907→\n   908→    /// Skip a peeked argument (used after checking with peek() and wanting to consume it).\n   909→    fn skip(self: *Self) void {\n   910→        if (self.index < self.args.len) {\n   911→            self.index += 1;\n   912→        }\n   913→    }\n   914→\n   915→    /// Check if current arg matches a flag, and if so consume it and return true.\n   916→    fn consumeFlag(self: *Self, short: ?[]const u8, long: []const u8) bool {\n   917→        const arg = self.peek() orelse return false;\n   918→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, long) or (short != null and std.mem.eql(u8, arg, short.?))) {\n   919→            self.skip();\n   920→            return true;\n   921→        }\n   922→        return false;\n   923→    }\n   924→\n   925→    /// Parse a u32 value after consuming a flag. Returns null if missing, error if invalid.\n   926→    fn consumeU32(self: *Self) ParseError!?u32 {\n   927→        const val = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n   928→        return std.fmt.parseInt(u32, val, 10) catch return error.InvalidArgument;\n   929→    }\n   930→\n   931→    /// Parse an optional --limit/-n flag, returning the value if present.\n   932→    fn parseLimitFlag(self: *Self) ParseError!?u32 {\n   933→        if (self.consumeFlag(\"-n\", \"--limit\")) {\n   934→            return try self.consumeU32();\n   935→        }\n   936→        return null;\n   937→    }\n   938→\n   939→    /// Returns the next arg if it's a positional (doesn't start with \"-\"), otherwise null.\n   940→    fn peekPositional(self: *Self) ?[]const u8 {\n   941→        const arg = self.peek() orelse return null;\n   942→        if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, arg, \"-\")) return null;\n   943→        return arg;\n   944→    }\n   945→};\n   946→\n   947→// Tests\n
