SelfDependency,\n    19→    CycleDetected,\n    20→    DependencyNotFound,\n    21→    IssueNotFound,\n    22→};\n    23→\n    24→pub const DependencyGraph = struct {\n    25→    store: *IssueStore,\n    26→    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n    27→\n    28→    const Self = @This();\n    29→\n    30→    pub fn init(store: *IssueStore, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) Self {\n    31→        return .{\n    32→            .store = store,\n    33→            .allocator = allocator,\n    34→        };\n    35→    }\n    36→\n    37→    /// Add a dependency (issue_id depends on depends_on_id).\n    38→    /// Returns error.SelfDependency if trying to depend on self.\n    39→    /// Returns error.CycleDetected if adding would create a cycle.\n    40→    pub fn addDependency(self: *Self, dep: Dependency) !void {\n    41→        // Check for self-dependency\n    42→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, dep.issue_id, dep.depends_on_id)) {\n    43→            return DependencyGraphError.SelfDependency;\n    44→        }\n    45→\n    46→        // Check if issue exists\n    47→        const issue = self.store.getRef(dep.issue_id) orelse\n    48→            return DependencyGraphError.IssueNotFound;\n    49→\n    50→        // Check for cycles before inserting\n    51→        if (try self.wouldCreateCycle(dep.issue_id, dep.depends_on_id)) {\n    52→            return DependencyGraphError.CycleDetected;\n    53→        }\n    54→\n    55→        // Check if dependency already exists\n    56→        for (issue.dependencies) |existing| {\n    57→            if (std.mem.eql(u8, existing.depends_on_id, dep.depends_on_id)) {\n    58→                return; // Already exists, no-op\n    59→            }\n    60→        }\n    61→\n    62→        // Clone and add the dependency\n    63→        const cloned = try cloneDependency(dep, self.allocator);\n    64→        errdefer freeDependency(@constCast(&cloned), self.allocator);\n    65→\n    66→        const new_deps = try self.allocator.alloc(Dependency, issue.dependencies.len + 1);\n    67→        @memcpy(new_deps[0..issue.dependencies.len], issue.dependencies);\n    68→        new_deps[issue.dependencies.len] = cloned;\n    69→\n    70→        // Only free the old array, not the dependency contents (they're now in new_deps)\n    71→        if (issue.dependencies.len > 0) {\n    72→            self.allocator.free(issue.dependencies);\n    73→        }\n    74→        issue.dependencies = new_deps;\n    75→\n    76→        try self.store.markDirty(dep.issue_id);\n    77→    }\n    78→\n    79→    /// Remove a dependency.\n    80→    pub fn removeDependency(self: *Self, issue_id: []const u8, depends_on_id: []const u8) !void {\n    81→        const issue = self.store.getRef(issue_id) orelse\n    82→            return DependencyGraphError.IssueNotFound;\n    83→\n    84→        var found_idx: ?usize = null;\n    85→        for (issue.dependencies, 0..) |dep, i| {\n    86→            if (std.mem.eql(u8, dep.depends_on_id, depends_on_id)) {\n    87→                found_idx = i;\n    88→                break;\n    89→            }\n    90→        }\n    91→\n    92→        if (found_idx) |fi| {\n    93→            freeDependency(@constCast(&issue.dependencies[fi]), self.allocator);\n    94→\n    95→            if (issue.dependencies.len == 1) {\n    96→                self.allocator.free(issue.dependencies);\n    97→                issue.dependencies = &[_]Dependency{};\n    98→            } else {\n    99→                const new_deps = try self.allocator.alloc(Dependency, issue.dependencies.len - 1);\n   100→                var j: usize = 0;\n   101→                for (issue.dependencies, 0..) |dep, i| {\n   102→                    if (i != fi) {\n   103→                        new_deps[j] = dep;\n   104→                        j += 1;\n   105→                    }\n   106→                }\n   107→                self.allocator.free(issue.dependencies);\n   108→                issue.dependencies = new_deps;\n   109→            }\n   110→\n   111→            try self.store.markDirty(issue_id);\n   112→        }\n   113→    }\n   114→\n   115→    /// Get dependencies for an issue (what it depends on).\n   116→    pub fn getDependencies(self: *Self, issue_id: []const u8) ![]Dependency {\n   117→        const issue = self.store.getRef(issue_id) orelse return &[_]Dependency{};\n   118→\n   119→        if (issue.dependencies.len == 0) return &[_]Dependency{};\n   120→\n   121→        const deps = try self.allocator.alloc(Dependency, issue.dependencies.len);\n   122→        errdefer self.allocator.free(deps);\n   123→\n   124→        for (issue.dependencies, 0..) |dep, i| {\n   125→            deps[i] = try cloneDependency(dep, self.allocator);\n   126→        }\n   127→\n   128→        return deps;\n   129→    }\n   130→\n   131→    /// Get dependents of an issue (what depends on it).\n   132→    pub fn getDependents(self: *Self, issue_id: []const u8) ![]Dependency {\n   133→        var deps: std.ArrayListUnmanaged(Dependency) = .{};\n   134→        errdefer {\n   135→            for (deps.items) |*dep| {\n   136→                freeDependency(dep, self.allocator);\n   137→            }\n   138→            deps.deinit(self.allocator);\n   139→        }\n   140→\n   141→        for 150→        return deps.toOwnedSlice(self.allocator);\n   151→    }\n   152→\n   153→    /// Check if adding a dependency would create a cycle.\n   154→    /// Uses DFS from depends_on_id to see if it can reach issue_id.\n   155→    pub fn wouldCreateCycle(self: *Self, issue_id: []const u8, depends_on_id: []const u8) !bool {\n   156→        var visited: std.StringHashMapUnmanaged(void) = .{};\n   157→        defer {\n   158→            var key_it = visited.keyIterator();\n   159→            while (key_it.next()) |key| {\n   160→                self.allocator.free(key.*);\n   161→            }\n   162→            visited.deinit(self.allocator);\n   163→        }\n   164→\n   165→        return try self.dfsReachable(depends_on_id, issue_id, &visited);\n   166→    }\n   167→\n   168→    fn dfsReachable(self: *Self, from: []const u8, target: []const u8, visited: *std.StringHashMapUnmanaged(void)) !bool {\n   169→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, from, target)) return true;\n   170→        if visited.put(self.allocator, from_copy, {});\n   175→\n   176→        const issue = self.store.getRef(from) orelse return false;\n   177→\n   178→        for (issue.dependencies) |dep| {\n   179→            if (try self.dfsReachable(dep.depends_on_id, target, visited)) {\n   180→                return true;\n   181→            }\n   182→        }\n   183→        return false;\n   184→    }\n   185→\n   186→    /// Detect all cycles in the dependency graph.\n   187→    /// Returns array of cycle paths, or null if no cycles.\n   188→    pub fn detectCycles(self: *Self) !?[][]const u8 {\n   189→        var all_issues: std.StringHashMapUnmanaged(void) = .{};\n   190→        defer {\n   191→            var it = all_issues.keyIterator();\n   192→            while (it.next()) |key| {\n   193→                self.allocator.free(key.*);\n   194→            }\n   195→            all_issues.deinit(self.allocator);\n   196→        }\n   197→\n   198→        // Collect all issue IDs involved in dependencies\n   199→        for (self.store.getAllRef()) |issue| {\n   200→            if (issue.dependencies.len > 0) {\n   201→                if (!all_issues.contains(issue.id)) {\n   202→                    const id_copy = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, issue.id);\n   203→                    try all_issues.put(self.allocator, id_copy, {});\n   204→                }\n   205→                for (issue.dependencies) |dep| {\n   206→                    if (!all_issues.contains(dep.depends_on_id)) {\n   207→                        const id_copy = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, dep.depends_on_id);\n   208→                        try all_issues.put(self.allocator, id_copy, {});\n   209→                    }\n   210→                }\n   211→            }\n   212→        }\n   213→\n   214→        var cycles: std.ArrayListUnmanaged([]const u8) = .{};\n   215→        errdefer {\n   216→            for (cycles.items) |c| {\n   217→                self.allocator.free(c);\n   218→            }\n   219→            cycles.deinit(self.allocator);\n   220→        }\n   221→\n   222→        var visited: std.StringHashMapUnmanaged(void) = .{};\n   223→        defer visited.deinit(self.allocator);\n   224→\n   225→        var rec_stack: std.StringHashMapUnmanaged(void) = .{};\n   226→        defer rec_stack.deinit(self.allocator);\n   227→\n   228→        var it = all_issues.keyIterator();\n   229→        while (it.next()) |key| {\n   230→            if (!visited.contains(key.*)) {\n   231→                var path: std.ArrayListUnmanaged([]const u8) = .{};\n   232→                defer path.deinit(self.allocator);\n   233→\n   234→                if (try self.detectCycleDfs(key.*, &visited, &rec_stack, &path)) {\n   235→                    const cycle_str = try std.mem.join(self.allocator, \" -> \", path.items);\n   236→                    try cycles.append(self.allocator, cycle_str);\n   237→                }\n   238→            }\n   239→        }\n   240→\n   241→        if (cycles.items.len == 0) {\n   242→            return null;\n   243→        }\n   244→\n   245→        return try cycles.toOwnedSlice(self.allocator);\n   246→    }\n   247→\n   248→    fn detectCycleDfs(\n   249→        self: *Self,\n   250→        node: []const u8,\n   251→        visited: *std.StringHashMapUnmanaged(void),\n   252→        rec_stack: *std.StringHashMapUnmanaged(void),\n   253→        path: *std.ArrayListUnmanaged([]const u8),\n   254→    ) !bool {\n   255→        try visited.put(self.allocator, node, {});\n   256→        try rec_stack.put(self.allocator, node, {});\n   257→        try path.append(self.allocator, node);\n   258→\n   259→        const issue = self.store.getRef(node) orelse {\n   260→            _ = path.pop();\n   261→            _ = rec_stack.remove(node);\n   262→            return false;\n   263→        };\n   264→\n   265→        for (issue.dependencies) |dep| {\n   266→            if (!visited.contains(dep.depends_on_id)) {\n   267→                if (try self.detectCycleDfs(dep.depends_on_id, visited, rec_stack, path)) {\n   268→                    return true;\n   269→                }\n   270→            } else if (rec_stack.contains(dep.depends_on_id)) {\n   271→                try path.append(self.allocator, dep.depends_on_id);\n   272→                return true;\n   273→            }\n   274→        }\n   275→\n   276→        _ = rec_stack.remove(node);\n   277→        _ = path.pop();\n   278→        return false;\n   279→    }\n   280→\n   281→    /// Get all issues that are ready (open, not blocked by open issues, not deferred).\n   282→    pub fn getReadyIssues(self: *Self) ![]Issue {\n   283→        const now = std.time.timestamp();\n   284→\n   285→        var results: std.ArrayListUnmanaged(Issue) = .{};\n   286→        errdefer {\n   287→            for (results.items) |*issue| {\n   288→                issue.deinit(self.allocator);\n   289→            }\n   290→            results.deinit(self.allocator);\n   291→        }\n   292→\n   293→        for (self.store.getAllRef()) |issue| {\n   294→            // Must be open\n   295→            if (!statusEql(issue.status, .open)) continue;\n   296→\n   297→            // Must not be deferred to future\n   298→            if (issue.defer_until.value) |defer_time| {\n   299→                if (issue.dependencies) |dep| {\n   305→                if (self.store.getRef(dep.depends_on_id)) |blocker| {\n   306→                    if (!statusEql(blocker.status, .closed) and\n   307→                        !statusEql(blocker.status, .tombstone))\n   308→                    {\n   309→                        has_open_blocker = true;\n   310→                        break;\n   311→                    }\n   312→                }\n   313→            }\n   314→            if (has_open_blocker) continue;\n   315→\n   316→            try results.append(self.allocator, try issue.clone(self.allocator));\n   317→        }\n   318→\n   319→        // Sort by priority then created_at\n   320→        std.mem.sortUnstable(Issue, results.items, {}, struct {\n   321→            fn lessThan(_: void, a: Issue, b: Issue) bool {\n   322→                if (a.priority.value != b.priority.value) {\n   323→                    return a.priority.value < b.priority.value;\n   324→                }\n   325→                return a.created_at.value < b.created_at.value;\n   326→            }\n   327→        }.lessThan);\n   328→\n   329→        return Dependency graph operations for beads_zig.\n//!\n//! Provides dependency management including:\n//! - Add/remove dependencies\n//! - Cycle detection (DFS algorithm)\n//! - Query dependencies and dependents\n//! - Ready/blocked issue queries\n\nconst std = @import(\"std\");\nconst store_mod = @import(\"store.zig\");\nconst IssueStore = store_mod.IssueStore;\nconst Issue = @import(\"../models/issue.zig\").Issue;\nconst Dependency = @import(\"../models/dependency.zig\").Dependency;\nconst DependencyType = @import(\"../models/dependency.zig\").DependencyType;\nconst Status = @import(\"../models/status.zig\").Status;\n\npub const DependencyGraphError = error{\n    SelfDependency,\n    CycleDetected,\n    DependencyNotFound,\n    IssueNotFound,\n};\n\npub const DependencyGraph = struct {\n    store: *IssueStore,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n\n    const Self = @This();\n\n    pub fn init(store: *IssueStore, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) Self {\n        return .{\n            .store = store,\n            .allocator = allocator,\n        };\n    }\n\n    /// Add a dependency (issue_id depends on depends_on_id).\n    /// Returns error.SelfDependency if trying to depend on self.\n    /// Returns error.CycleDetected if adding would create a cycle.\n    pub fn addDependency(self: *Self, dep: Dependency) !void {\n        // Check for self-dependency\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, dep.issue_id, dep.depends_on_id)) {\n            return DependencyGraphError.SelfDependency;\n        }\n\n        // Check if issue exists\n        const issue = self.store.getRef(dep.issue_id) orelse\n            return DependencyGraphError.IssueNotFound;\n\n        // Check for cycles before inserting\n        if (try self.wouldCreateCycle(dep.issue_id, dep.depends_on_id)) {\n            return DependencyGraphError.CycleDetected;\n        }\n\n        // Check if dependency already exists\n        for (issue.dependencies) |existing| {\n            if (std.mem.eql(u8, existing.depends_on_id, dep.depends_on_id)) {\n                return; // Already exists, no-op\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Clone and add the dependency\n        const cloned = try cloneDependency(dep, self.allocator);\n        errdefer freeDependency(@constCast(&cloned), self.allocator);\n\n        const new_deps = try self.allocator.alloc(Dependency, issue.dependencies.len + 1);\n        @memcpy(new_deps[0..issue.dependencies.len], issue.dependencies);\n        new_deps[issue.dependencies.len] = cloned;\n\n        // Only free the old array, not the dependency contents (they're now in new_deps)\n        if (issue.dependencies.len > 0) {\n            self.allocator.free(issue.dependencies);\n        }\n        issue.dependencies = new_deps;\n\n        try self.store.markDirty(dep.issue_id);\n    }\n\n    /// Remove a dependency.\n    pub fn removeDependency(self: *Self, issue_id: []const u8, depends_on_id: []const u8) !void {\n        const issue = self.store.getRef(issue_id) orelse\n            return DependencyGraphError.IssueNotFound;\n\n        var found_idx: ?usize = null;\n        for (issue.dependencies, 0..) |dep, i| {\n            if (std.mem.eql(u8, dep.depends_on_id, depends_on_id)) {\n                found_idx = i;\n                break;\n            }\n        }\n\n        if (found_idx) |fi| {\n            freeDependency(@constCast(&issue.dependencies[fi]), self.allocator);\n\n            if (issue.dependencies.len == 1) {\n                self.allocator.free(issue.dependencies);\n                issue.dependencies = &[_]Dependency{};\n            } else {\n                const new_deps = try self.allocator.alloc(Dependency, issue.dependencies.len - 1);\n                var j: usize = 0;\n                for (issue.dependencies, 0..) |dep, i| {\n                    if (i != fi) {\n                        new_deps[j] = dep;\n                        j += 1;\n                    }\n                }\n                self.allocator.free(issue.dependencies);\n                issue.dependencies = new_deps;\n            }\n\n            try self.store.markDirty(issue_id);\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Get dependencies for an issue (what it depends on).\n    pub fn getDependencies(self: *Self, issue_id: []const u8) ![]Dependency {\n        const issue = self.store.getRef(issue_id) orelse return &[_]Dependency{};\n\n        if (issue.dependencies.len == 0) return &[_]Dependency{};\n\n        const deps = try self.allocator.alloc(Dependency, issue.dependencies.len);\n        errdefer self.allocator.free(deps);\n\n        for (issue.dependencies, 0..) |dep, i| {\n            deps[i] = try cloneDependency(dep, self.allocator);\n        }\n\n        return deps;\n    }\n\n    /// Get dependents of an issue (what depends on it).\n    pub fn getDependents(self: *Self, issue_id: []const u8) ![]Dependency {\n        var deps: std.ArrayListUnmanaged(Dependency) = .{};\n        errdefer {\n            for (deps.items) |*dep| {\n                freeDependency(dep, self.allocator);\n            }\n            deps.deinit(self.allocator);\n        }\n\n        for (self.store.getAllRef()) |issue| {\n            for (issue.dependencies) |dep| {\n                if (std.mem.eql(u8, dep.depends_on_id, issue_id)) {\n                    const cloned = try cloneDependency(dep, self.allocator);\n                    try deps.append(self.allocator, cloned);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        return deps.toOwnedSlice(self.allocator);\n    }\n\n    /// Check if adding a dependency would create a cycle.\n    /// Uses DFS from depends_on_id to see if it can reach issue_id.\n    pub fn wouldCreateCycle(self: *Self, issue_id: []const u8, depends_on_id: []const u8) !bool {\n        var visited: std.StringHashMapUnmanaged(void) = .{};\n        defer {\n            var key_it = visited.keyIterator();\n            while (key_it.next()) |key| {\n                self.allocator.free(key.*);\n            }\n            visited.deinit(self.allocator);\n        }\n\n        return try self.dfsReachable(depends_on_id, issue_id, &visited);\n    }\n\n    fn dfsReachable(self: *Self, from: []const u8, target: []const u8, visited: *std.StringHashMapUnmanaged(void)) !bool {\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, from, target)) return true;\n        if (visited.contains(from)) return false;\n\n        const from_copy = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, from);\n        errdefer self.allocator.free(from_copy);\n        try visited.put(self.allocator, from_copy, {});\n\n        const issue = self.store.getRef(from) orelse return false;\n\n        for (issue.dependencies) |dep| {\n            if (try self.dfsReachable(dep.depends_on_id, target, visited)) {\n                return true;\n            }\n        }\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    /// Detect all cycles in the dependency graph.\n    /// Returns array of cycle paths, or null if no cycles.\n    pub fn detectCycles(self: *Self) !?[][]const u8 {\n        var all_issues: std.StringHashMapUnmanaged(void) = .{};\n        defer {\n            var it = all_issues.keyIterator();\n            while (it.next()) |key| {\n                self.allocator.free(key.*);\n            }\n            all_issues.deinit(self.allocator);\n        }\n\n        // Collect all issue IDs involved in dependencies\n        for (self.store.getAllRef()) |issue| {\n            if (issue.dependencies.len > 0) {\n                if (!all_issues.contains(issue.id)) {\n                    const id_copy = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, issue.id);\n                    try all_issues.put(self.allocator, id_copy, {});\n                }\n                for (issue.dependencies) |dep| {\n                    if (!all_issues.contains(dep.depends_on_id)) {\n                        const id_copy = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, dep.depends_on_id);\n                        try all_issues.put(self.allocator, id_copy, {});\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        var cycles: std.ArrayListUnmanaged([]const u8) = .{};\n        errdefer {\n            for (cycles.items) |c| {\n                self.allocator.free(c);\n            }\n            cycles.deinit(self.allocator);\n        }\n\n        var visited: std.StringHashMapUnmanaged(void) = .{};\n        defer visited.deinit(self.allocator);\n\n        var rec_stack: std.StringHashMapUnmanaged(void) = .{};\n        defer rec_stack.deinit(self.allocator);\n\n        var it = all_issues.keyIterator();\n        while (it.next()) |key| {\n            if (!visited.contains(key.*)) {\n                var path: std.ArrayListUnmanaged([]const u8) = .{};\n                defer path.deinit(self.allocator);\n\n                if (try self.detectCycleDfs(key.*, &visited, &rec_stack, &path)) {\n                    const cycle_str = try std.mem.join(self.allocator, \" -> \", path.items);\n                    try cycles.append(self.allocator, cycle_str);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        if (cycles.items.len == 0) {\n            return null;\n        }\n\n        return try cycles.toOwnedSlice(self.allocator);\n    }\n\n    fn detectCycleDfs(\n        self: *Self,\n        node: []const u8,\n        visited: *std.StringHashMapUnmanaged(void),\n        rec_stack: *std.StringHashMapUnmanaged(void),\n        path: *std.ArrayListUnmanaged([]const u8),\n    ) !bool {\n        try visited.put(self.allocator, node, {});\n        try rec_stack.put(self.allocator, node, {});\n        try path.append(self.allocator, node);\n\n        const issue = self.store.getRef(node) orelse {\n            _ = path.pop();\n            _ = rec_stack.remove(node);\n            return false;\n        };\n\n        for (issue.dependencies) |dep| {\n            if (!visited.contains(dep.depends_on_id)) {\n                if (try self.detectCycleDfs(dep.depends_on_id, visited, rec_stack, path)) {\n                    return true;\n                }\n            } else if (rec_stack.contains(dep.depends_on_id)) {\n                try path.append(self.allocator, dep.depends_on_id);\n                return true;\n            }\n        }\n\n        _ = rec_stack.remove(node);\n        _ = path.pop();\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    /// Get all issues that are ready (open, not blocked by open issues, not deferred).\n    pub fn getReadyIssues(self: *Self) ![]Issue {\n        const now = std.time.timestamp();\n\n        var results: std.ArrayListUnmanaged(Issue) = .{};\n        errdefer {\n            for (results.items) |*issue| {\n                issue.deinit(self.allocator);\n            }\n            results.deinit(self.allocator);\n        }\n\n        for (self.store.getAllRef()) |issue| {\n            // Must be open\n            if (!statusEql(issue.status, .open)) continue;\n\n            // Must not be deferred to future\n            if (issue.defer_until.value) |defer_time| {\n                if (defer_time > now) continue;\n            }\n\n            // Must not have any open blockers\n            var has_open_blocker = false;\n            for (issue.dependencies) |dep| {\n                if (self.store.getRef(dep.depends_on_id)) |blocker| {\n                    if (!statusEql(blocker.status, .closed) and\n                        !statusEql(blocker.status, .tombstone))\n                    {\n                        has_open_blocker = true;\n                        break;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n            if (has_open_blocker) continue;\n\n            try results.append(self.allocator, try issue.clone(self.allocator));\n        }\n\n        // Sort by priority then created_at\n        std.mem.sortUnstable(Issue, results.items, {}, struct {\n            fn lessThan(_: void, a: Issue, b: Issue) bool {\n                if (a.priority.value != b.priority.value) {\n                    return a.priority.value < b.priority.value;\n                }\n                return a.created_at.value < b.created_at.value;\n            }\n        }.lessThan);\n\n        return results.toOwnedSlice(self.allocator);\n    }\n\n    /// Get all blocked issues (open issues with unresolved dependencies).\n    pub fn getBlockedIssues(self: *Self) ![]Issue {\n        var results: std.ArrayListUnmanaged(Issue) = .{};\n        errdefer {\n            for (results.items) |*issue| {\n                issue.deinit(self.allocator);\n            }\n            results.deinit(self.allocator);\n        }\n\n        for (self.store.getAllRef()) |issue| {\n            // Must be open\n            if (!statusEql(issue.status, .open)) continue;\n\n            // Must have at least one open blocker\n            var has_open_blocker = false;\n            for (issue.dependencies) |dep| {\n                if (self.store.getRef(dep.depends_on_id)) |blocker| {\n                    if (!statusEql(blocker.status, .closed) and\n                        !statusEql(blocker.status, .tombstone))\n                    {\n                        has_open_blocker = true;\n                        break;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n            if (!has_open_blocker) continue;\n\n            try results.append(self.allocator, try issue.clone(self.allocator));\n        }\n\n        // Sort by priority then created_at\n        std.mem.sortUnstable(Issue, results.items, {}, struct {\n            fn lessThan(_: void, a: Issue, b: Issue) bool {\n                if (a.priority.value != b.priority.value) {\n                    return a.priority.value < b.priority.value;\n                }\n                return a.created_at.value < b.created_at.value;\n            }\n        }.lessThan);\n\n        return results.toOwnedSlice(self.allocator);\n    }\n\n    /// Get blockers for tag_a: Tag = a;\n    const tag_b: Tag = b;\n    if (tag_a != tag_b) return false;\n    return if (tag_a == .custom) std.mem.eql(u8, a.custom, b.custom) else true;\n}\n\nfn cloneDependency(dep: Dependency, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) !Dependency {\n    var result: Dependency = undefined;\n\n    result.issue_id = try allocator.dupe(u8, dep.issue_id);\n    errdefer (dep.created_by) |c| try allocator.dupe(u8, c) else null;\n    result.metadata = if (dep.metadata) |m| try allocator.dupe(u8, m) else null;\n    result.thread_id = if (dep.thread_id) |t| try allocator.dupe(u8, t) else null;\n\n    return result;\n}\n\nfn freeDependency(dep: *Dependency, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) void {\n    allocator.free(dep.issue_id);\n
